KubeSolver

Welcome to the homepage of a project KubeSolver.

From this page you can download KubeSolver. The command line tool to generate algorithms for 3x3 Rubik cube.

Read the documentation and changelog

Download Windows executable from here KubeSolver 1.0.4.

MAC OS version can be downloaded from here KubeSolver for mac OS.

set_gen RUD
R2 D L2 D F2 L D R' D2 L D' R' U2
reconstruct
